 Pakistan Prime Minister Nawaz Sharif today said that former President Pervez Musharraf will be prosecuted for gross treason for violating the country's constitution twice
 doshi qaraar die jane par musharraf ko maut kii sajaa athwa umrakaid ho sakati he
 Two of the cases the Prime Minister has mentioned are the 1999 coup and the second is the dismissal of judges by imposing emergency in 2007
 sharif ne sansad ke nichle sadan neshnal essembly main yah elaan apane satta main lautne ke teen saptaah baad kiya he
 Sharif told Parliament that the steps taken by Musharraf came under the purview of 'gross treason'
 unhone kaha ki musharraf ko unke kadamon ke liye supreme court main sunwaayee kaa saamana karnaa chahie
 Referring to Musharraf's decision to impose emergency in 2007, Sharif said, "it is a firm view of the federal government that on November 3, 2007, the steps taken to circumvent the constitution under gross treason under Article 6 of the Constitution of Pakistan" Comes
 piemail-en ke netaa sharif ne kaha, pradhanmantri samvidhan kii hifaazat karne kii shapath letaa he
 This oath implied that the government would bring the culprits to justice under Article 6
 sharif ne kaha ki unki sarkaar musharraf ke khilaaf mukadmaa chalaane ke sandarbh main sabhi raajnneetik dalon ko vishwaas main lene ke liye vichaar-vimarsh karegi
 Immediately after Sharif's statement in Parliament, Attorney General Munir Malik informed the bench of the Supreme Court about the government's position, which is hearing a petition seeking a case of gross treason against Musharraf
 atarni general kaa kahana he ki musharraf ke khilaaf mukadmaa chalaane kii prakriya aarambh ho chuki he, haalanki sarkaar ko apane bhavishya ke kadam ke liye 30 dinon ke samay kii jarurat he
 On the other hand, Pakistan's largest court gave the Attorney General just three days to decide the future course of action and ordered them to file their reply by Thursday
 jaankaron kaa kahana he ki sarkaar ko sena kii taraf se dabaav kaa saamana karnaa pad saktaa he, kyonki vah apane ek purv general ko saarvajanik rup se apamaanit hote nahin dekhnaa chaahegi
 The comments pakistan ke samvidhan ke anusaar, rashtradroh ke maamle main mukademe kaa faisla sirf sarkaar kar sakati he 
 Musharraf violated the Constitution twice, Sharif said
 1999 main unhone nirvaachit sarkaar kaa takhtapalat kiya
 He then dismissed the judges and placed them under house arrest

 PML-N leader Sharif said, the Prime Minister takes an oath to defend the Constitution

 sansad main sharif ke bayaan ke tatkaal baad atarni general munir malik ne sarkaar kii sthiti ke bare main supreme court kii us peeth ko suchit kiya, jo musharraf ke khilaaf ghor rashtradroh kaa maamla chalaane kii maang sambandhi yachika par sunwaayee kar rahi he
 The Attorney General says that the process of prosecuting Musharraf has begun, although the government needs 30 days for its future action
 udhar, pakistan kii sabase badi adaalat ne etorni general ko bhavishya ke kadam ke bare main faisle ke mahaj teen din kaa samay diya tathaa unhen aadesh diya ki sarkaar guuruuvaar tak apana jawaab daakhil kare
 Experts say the government may have to face pressure from the military, as it would not like to see one of its former generals being publicly humiliated
 tippaniyan According to Pakistan's constitution, only the government can decide the case in case of treason
 sharif ne kaha, musharraf ne do baar samvidhan kaa ulanghan kiya
 In 1999, he overthrew the elected government

 The Budgam resident, who has managed to get a hall ticket for his brown cow to appear in the professional entrance examination, says that he is determined to take his cow to take the exam
 abdul raashid bhatta ne samvaadadaataaon se kaha, 'aap aamantrit hai
 It is my legal right to take my cow for examination
 maine fees bhari he, isliye gaay ko vahaan le janaa meraa adhikaar he
 Bhatt, who hails from Chadura area of central Kashmir's Budgam district, said, "my intention was not to hurt anyone's feelings or make fun of anyone
" maine yah form sirf vyavastha ko parakhane ke liye bharaa
 ' jammu and kashmir board of profeshnal entrens ejamination (biopii) kii online panjikaran vyavastha kii khaamiyon ko ujagar karne ke prayaas ke tahat bhatta apni gaay ke liye pravesh pariksha kaa pravesh patr hasil karne main safal rahe the
 This entrance exam is for admission to the diploma course of Polytechnic College
 pravesh patr board dwaara kachir gau (bhuri gaay) ke naam par jari kiya gaya, jise ki gura daand (laal bail) kii beti bataaya gaya tha
 The cow has been allotted a seat at the Government Degree College in Bemina to sit for the entrance examination to be held on May 10
 bhatta ne kaha ki biopii kii maujuuda vyavastha kisi ko bhi pariksha ke liye panjikaran karne detii he
 He said, 'you also know how the BOPEE examinations are conducted - any cow, calf or buffalo can also participate in it
 maine ek gaay ke liye form bharke dekhne ke bare main sochaa or maine fees bharne ke saath-saath sabhi aupchaariktaayen puri kar deen
 Comments pravesh pariksha main baithne ke liye ek aavedak kaa kisi manyata praapt board se metriculation kii pariksha main paas hona jaruri hota he
 However, people appearing in matriculation examination can also appear for entrance examination
 pravesh ke liye unka metriculation pariksha main paas hona jaruri hota he
 With a sarcastic smile on his face, Bhatt said, 'the result of my cow is yet to come

 ' In an effort to highlight the flaws in the online registration system of the Jammu and Kashmir Board of Professional Entrance Examination (BOPEE), Bhatt was successful in getting the entrance exam for his cow
 yah pravesh pariksha polytechnic college ke diploma course main pravesh ke liye he
 The admit card was issued by the board in the name of Kachir Gau (brown cow), who was said to be the daughter of Goora Dand (red bull)
 10 may ko hone vaali pravesh pariksha main baithne ke liye is gaay ko bemina sthit sarkari degree college main seat aavantit kii gai he

 'tippaniyan For appearing in the entrance examination, an applicant must pass the examination of matriculation from a recognized board

 Know, political journey of Pappu Yadav
 
 
 1
 Rajesh Ranjan alias Pappu Yadav was born on 24 December 1967 in Khurda Karveli village of Purnia district of Bihar
 2
 He did his schooling in Supaul and then graduated from BN Mandal University Madhepura
 3
 Also did diploma from IGNOU on Disaster Management and Human Rights
 4
 Pappu Yadav married Ranjit Ranjan, who is currently a Congress MP
 5
 In 1990, he became an MLA for the first time by winning the Bihar Assembly elections as an independent candidate
 6
 In 1991, he contested the 10th Lok Sabha and won from Purnia seat
 7
 He was also a member of SP, LJP and RJD
 7 may 2015 ko argedy me party virdohi gatividhiyon kaa hawala dete hue unhen suspend kar diya
 8
 1998 main pappu yadav par CPI-M netaa ajit sarkaar kii hatya kaa aarope laga or vah 1999 main giraftaar kar liye gaye
 9

 10

 11

 12
 17 may 2013 ko patna hoicourt ne paryaapt saboot na hone kii baat kehete hue pappu yadav ko jail se reeha karne aadesh diya
 13

 vah apni patni or bacchon ke saath shankar singh waghela ke ghar par hi rahata tha

 iske baad vah waapas nahin lautaa
